\mbox{\Hypertarget{raylib_8h_abf00b975992bc5978bd579b9e5de2e38}\label{raylib_8h_abf00b975992bc5978bd579b9e5de2e38}} 
\index{raylib.h@{raylib.h}!RAYLIB\_VERSION@{RAYLIB\_VERSION}}
\index{RAYLIB\_VERSION@{RAYLIB\_VERSION}!raylib.h@{raylib.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RAYLIB\_VERSION}{RAYLIB\_VERSION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define RAYLIB\+\_\+\+VERSION~\char`\"{}4.\+5-\/dev\char`\"{}}



raylib v4.\+5-\/dev -\/ A simple and easy-\/to-\/use library to enjoy videogames programming (www.\+raylib.\+com) 

FEATURES\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item NO external dependencies, all required libraries included with raylib
\item Multiplatform\+: Windows, Linux, Free\+BSD, Open\+BSD, Net\+BSD, Dragon\+Fly, Mac\+OS, Haiku, Android, Raspberry Pi, DRM native, HTML5.
\item Written in plain C code (C99) in Pascal\+Case/camel\+Case notation
\item Hardware accelerated with Open\+GL (1.\+1, 2.\+1, 3.\+3, 4.\+3 or ES2 -\/ choose at compile)
\item Unique Open\+GL abstraction layer (usable as standalone module)\+: \mbox{[}rlgl\mbox{]}
\item Multiple Fonts formats supported (TTF, XNA fonts, Angel\+Code fonts)
\item Outstanding texture formats support, including compressed formats (DXT, ETC, ASTC)
\item Full 3d support for 3d Shapes, Models, Billboards, Heightmaps and more!
\item Flexible Materials system, supporting classic maps and PBR maps
\item Animated 3D models supported (skeletal bones animation) (IQM)
\item Shaders support, including \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_model}{Model}} shaders and Postprocessing shaders
\item Powerful math module for Vector, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_matrix}{Matrix}} and Quaternion operations\+: \mbox{[}raymath\mbox{]}
\item Audio loading and playing with streaming support (WAV, OGG, MP3, FLAC, XM, MOD)
\item VR stereo rendering with configurable HMD device parameters
\item Bindings to multiple programming languages available!
\end{DoxyItemize}

NOTES\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item One default \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_font}{Font}} is loaded on \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_8h_a0cf9b0ddf8b9e2939b24085ed0d208c3}{Init\+Window()}}-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}Load\+Font\+Default() \mbox{[}core, text\mbox{]}
\item One default Texture2D is loaded on rlgl\+Init(), 1x1 white pixel R8\+G8\+B8\+A8 \mbox{[}rlgl\mbox{]} (Open\+GL 3.\+3 or ES2)
\item One default \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_shader}{Shader}} is loaded on rlgl\+Init()-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}rl\+Load\+Shader\+Default() \mbox{[}rlgl\mbox{]} (Open\+GL 3.\+3 or ES2)
\item One default Render\+Batch is loaded on rlgl\+Init()-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}rl\+Load\+Render\+Batch() \mbox{[}rlgl\mbox{]} (Open\+GL 3.\+3 or ES2)
\end{DoxyItemize}

DEPENDENCIES (included)\+: \mbox{[}rcore\mbox{]} rglfw (Camilla Lwy -\/ github.\+com/glfw/glfw) for window/context management and input (PLATFORM\+\_\+\+DESKTOP) \mbox{[}rlgl\mbox{]} glad (David Herberth -\/ github.\+com/\+Dav1dde/glad) for Open\+GL 3.\+3 extensions loading (PLATFORM\+\_\+\+DESKTOP) \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} miniaudio (David Reid -\/ github.\+com/mackron/miniaudio) for audio device/context management

OPTIONAL DEPENDENCIES (included)\+: \mbox{[}rcore\mbox{]} msf\+\_\+gif (Miles Fogle) for GIF recording \mbox{[}rcore\mbox{]} sinfl (Micha Mettke) for DEFLATE decompression algorithm \mbox{[}rcore\mbox{]} sdefl (Micha Mettke) for DEFLATE compression algorithm \mbox{[}rtextures\mbox{]} stb\+\_\+image (Sean Barret) for images loading (BMP, TGA, PNG, JPEG, HDR...) \mbox{[}rtextures\mbox{]} stb\+\_\+image\+\_\+write (Sean Barret) for image writing (BMP, TGA, PNG, JPG) \mbox{[}rtextures\mbox{]} stb\+\_\+image\+\_\+resize (Sean Barret) for image resizing algorithms \mbox{[}rtext\mbox{]} stb\+\_\+truetype (Sean Barret) for ttf fonts loading \mbox{[}rtext\mbox{]} stb\+\_\+rect\+\_\+pack (Sean Barret) for rectangles packing \mbox{[}rmodels\mbox{]} par\+\_\+shapes (Philip Rideout) for parametric 3d shapes generation \mbox{[}rmodels\mbox{]} tinyobj\+\_\+loader\+\_\+c (Syoyo Fujita) for models loading (OBJ, MTL) \mbox{[}rmodels\mbox{]} cgltf (Johannes Kuhlmann) for models loading (gl\+TF) \mbox{[}rmodels\mbox{]} Model3D (bzt) for models loading (M3D, \href{https://bztsrc.gitlab.io/model3d}{\texttt{ https\+://bztsrc.\+gitlab.\+io/model3d}}) \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} dr\+\_\+wav (David Reid) for WAV audio file loading \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} dr\+\_\+flac (David Reid) for FLAC audio file loading \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} dr\+\_\+mp3 (David Reid) for MP3 audio file loading \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} stb\+\_\+vorbis (Sean Barret) for OGG audio loading \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} jar\+\_\+xm (Joshua Reisenauer) for XM audio module loading \mbox{[}raudio\mbox{]} jar\+\_\+mod (Joshua Reisenauer) for MOD audio module loading
